of Low Sensor Battery Level\r\n  * Email Alarm\r\n\r\nDisplay Mode:\r\n  *Meter View\r\n  *Dashboard\r\n  *HMI (Human Machine Interface)\r\n  *Data Listing\r\n  *Chart Comparison\r\n\r\n[Direct Mode]\r\nG7 Wireless Client receives data from G7 Base Station directly, and displays in user friendly graphics interface.\r\n\r\n[Server Mode]\r\n1. G7 wireless sensors send temperature and humidity reading to G7 Base Station through wireless radio frequency. \r\n2. Base Station uploads reading data to G7 Server over LAN/Internet. \r\n3. G7 Server saves data into its database in MySQL/SQL/Oracle.\r\n4. G7 Wireless Client accesses data from G7 Server System over LAN/Internet and displays in user friendly graphics interface.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Les plus populaires","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;mostPopular;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":994,"PageSize":200}}
